<section class="services" id="services">
<div class="container">

<div class="section-header wow fadeIn animated animated" data-wow-offset="10" data-wow-duration="1.5s" style="visibility: visible; animation-duration: 1.5s; animation-name: fadeIn;">

<h2 class="dark-text">FAQ</h2>
<div class="colored-line">
</div>
<div class="section-description">
Our most frequently asked questions
</div>
<div class="colored-line">
</div>
</div>

<div class="row">

<div class="col-md-4 single-service wow fadeIn animated animated" data-wow-offset="10" data-wow-duration="1.5s" style="visibility: visible; animation-duration: 1.5s; animation-name: fadeIn;">

<h3>How do I share my files?</h3>

<p><strong>Simple</strong>.<br /> Either drag &amp; drop them into our uploader, or click the upload box to select your file. Once the upload is complete, we will issue you a unique URL which you can share with others who can then download the file instantly.</p>
</div>


<div class="col-md-4 single-service wow fadeIn animated animated" data-wow-offset="10" data-wow-duration="1.5s" style="visibility: visible; animation-duration: 1.5s; animation-name: fadeIn;">

<h3>How long will my files be online?</h3>

<p><strong>Up to 30 days for guests, forever for registered users</strong>. <br />
You can also upload files and set them to auto expire after 1 hour, 1 day, 7 days, or 30 days.</p>
<p>Registered users can store their files forever, as well as create one time download links.</p>
</div>


<div class="col-md-4 single-service wow fadeIn animated animated" data-wow-offset="10" data-wow-duration="1.5s" style="visibility: visible; animation-duration: 1.5s; animation-name: fadeIn;">

<h3>What can I upload?</h3>

<p><strong>Anything</strong>. <br />Just keep it legal. Uploadfiles.io was built with love, to allow everybody to be able to share their files.</p>
<p> We'll be able to keep offering the service as long as the files shared aren't breaking any laws.</p>
</div>

</div>

<div class="row">

<div class="col-md-4 single-service wow fadeIn animated animated" data-wow-offset="10" data-wow-duration="1.5s" style="visibility: visible; animation-duration: 1.5s; animation-name: fadeIn;">

<h3>Can I email my files?</h3>

<p><strong>Yes</strong>.<br /> You can of course email your file URLs, however we do not offer an email service directly (yet). Instead you can use our "Add this" plugin or you can simply copy the URL into your email client.</p>
</div>


<div class="col-md-4 single-service wow fadeIn animated animated" data-wow-offset="10" data-wow-duration="1.5s" style="visibility: visible; animation-duration: 1.5s; animation-name: fadeIn;">

<h3>Is Uploadfiles.io really free?</h3>

<p><strong>Yes</strong>. <br />The core service is completely free, <br />there are no hidden costs to host your files.</p>
<p>We have paid plans for advanced features, but the service will always remain free to use.</p>
</div>


<div class="col-md-4 single-service wow fadeIn animated animated" data-wow-offset="10" data-wow-duration="1.5s" style="visibility: visible; animation-duration: 1.5s; animation-name: fadeIn;">

<h3>How do I download a file?</h3>

<p><strong>Click download</strong>. <br />It's very easy (yet we still get asked this a lot). When you've been sent a file URL, simply click the "download" button. Free users will need to wait a few seconds before the button will be available. </p>
</div>

</div>

<div class="row">

<div class="col-md-4 single-service wow fadeIn animated animated" data-wow-offset="10" data-wow-duration="1.5s" style="visibility: visible; animation-duration: 1.5s; animation-name: fadeIn;">

<h3>Why was my file removed?</h3>

<p><strong>Complaints</strong>. <br />Files must adhere to our <a href="/terms">terms of service</a> in order to remain hosted on Uploadfiles, repeatedly reported files will be automatically removed. </p>
</div>


<div class="col-md-4 single-service wow fadeIn animated animated" data-wow-offset="10" data-wow-duration="1.5s" style="visibility: visible; animation-duration: 1.5s; animation-name: fadeIn;">

<h3>How many downloads per file?</h3>

<p><strong>Unlimited</strong>. <br />We do not impose bandwidth limits, your uploads can be continuously downloaded until the file is either deleted, or it expires.</p>
</div>


<div class="col-md-4 single-service wow fadeIn animated animated" data-wow-offset="10" data-wow-duration="1.5s" style="visibility: visible; animation-duration: 1.5s; animation-name: fadeIn;">

<h3>Are there log files or backups?</h3>

<p><strong>No</strong>. <br />All uploads are completely anonymous, our logs are cycled continuously. Once a file has automatically been deleted, it is completely gone, forever.</p>
</div>

</div>

</div>

</section>
